Wikidata [g]\")\n\nAppearance\n\nmove to sidebar hide\n\nFrom Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia\n\nTaiwanese rock band\n\n\"Cao Dong\" redirects here. For other uses, see [Cao Dong (disambiguation)](/wiki/Cao_Dong_\\(disambiguation\\) \"Cao Dong (disambiguation)\").\n\nNo Party For Cao Dong\n\n[![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/No_Party_For_Cao_Dong_in_2023.jpg/250px-No_Party_For_Cao_Dong_in_2023.jpg)](/wiki/File:No_Party_For_Cao_Dong_in_2023.jpg)\n\nBackground information\n\nOrigin\n\n[Taiwan](/wiki/Taiwan \"Taiwan\")\n\nGenres\n\n-   [alternative rock](/wiki/Alternative_rock \"Alternative rock\")\n-   [indie rock](/wiki/Indie_rock \"Indie rock\")\n-   [post-rock](/wiki/Post-rock \"Post-rock\")\n-   [grunge](/wiki/Grunge \"Grunge\")\n\nYears active\n\n2012-present\n\nMembers\n\n-   Wood Lin\n-   Judy Chan (Chu Chu)\n-   Sam Yang\n-   Huang Shih-wei\n\nPast members\n\n-   Sam Cheng\n-   Leo Liu\n-   Fan Tsai\n\nChinese name\n\n[Traditional Chinese](/wiki/Traditional_Chinese_characters \"Traditional Chinese characters\")\n\n草東沒有派對\n\n[Simplified Chinese](/wiki/Simplified_Chinese_characters \"Simplified Chinese characters\")\n\n草东没有派对\n\nTranscriptions\n\n[Standard Mandarin](/wiki/Standard_Chinese \"Standard Chinese\")\n\n[Hanyu Pinyin](/wiki/Hanyu_Pinyin \"Hanyu Pinyin\")\n\nCǎo Dōng Méiyǒu Pàiduì\n\n[Bopomofo](/wiki/Bopomofo \"Bopomofo\")\n\nㄘㄠˇㄉㄨㄥㄇㄟˊㄧㄡˇㄆㄞˋㄉㄨㄟˋ\n\n**No Party For Cao Dong** ([Chinese](/wiki/Traditional_Chinese_characters \"Traditional Chinese characters\"): 草東沒有派對) is a Taiwanese [indie rock](/wiki/Indie_rock \"Indie rock\") band currently consisting of Wood Lin (vocals and guitar), Judy Chan (guitar), Sam Yang (bass), and Huang Shih-wei (drums).\n\n## History\n\n\\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=No_Party_for_Cao_Dong&action=edit&section=1 \"Edit section: History\")\\]\n\n### 2012–2014: Formation\n\n\\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=No_Party_for_Cao_Dong&action=edit&section=2 \"Edit section: 2012–2014: Formation\")\\]\n\nGuitarists and vocalists Wood Lin and Judy Chan met each other in high school, and remained friends during their days at [Taipei National University of the Arts](/wiki/Taipei_National_University_of_the_Arts \"Taipei National University of the Arts\"). In 2012, they started a band with schoolmates Lee You on bass and Huang Shih-Wei on drums, naming it Party at Cao Dong Street (草東街派對) after [the eponymous road](/w/index.php?title=Caodong_Street&action=edit&redlink=1 \"Caodong Street (page does not exist)\") \\[[zh](https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E6%9D%B1%E8%A1%97 \"zh:草東街\")\\] in [Shilin District](/wiki/Shilin_District \"Shilin District\"), [Taipei](/wiki/Taipei \"Taipei\"), where they often hung out; Lin would skateboard there while Chan would run alongside him, accompanying him to lose weight.[\\[1\\]](#cite_note-1) Initially, they played a style of electronic rock under the influence of [Two Door Cinema Club](/wiki/Two_Door_Cinema_Club \"Two Door Cinema Club\"), and performed at various events within and out of their campus.[\\[2\\]](#cite_note-blow-2)\n\nFollowing a series of lineup changes which saw the departures of Lee and Huang, the remaining members decided to rename the band No Party for Cao Dong in 2014, and enlisted FUBAR frontman Sam Cheng and Leo Liu to fill the bass and drum spots respectively. The band would then upload their original tracks \"Old Zhang\", \"Grisly Me\" and \"Fifty\" on the Internet. It was at that time when Cheng was conscripted for military service, as such they took a hiatus for nearly a year. During this period, the band started to adopt a different attitude towards their later works and consider making music seriously, hence in early 2015, they recruited fellow Taipei National University of the Arts graduate Sam Yang to take Cheng's place on bass.[\\[2\\]](#cite_note-blow-2) Cheng, meanwhile, returned to his previous band FUBAR, which had since been renamed to Grey Dwarf Star from 2016 and Deca Joins since 2017.\\[*[citation needed](/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed \"Wikipedia:Citation needed\")*\\]\n\n### 2015–2017: *The Servile* and rise to popularity\n\n\\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=No_Party_for_Cao_Dong&action=edit&section=3 \"Edit section: 2015–2017: The Servile and rise to popularity\")\\]\n\nIn 2015, the band self-released an EP which sold out in a single day.[\\[3\\]](#cite_note-billboard-golden-3) On May 20, they made their return to the stage with their first major concert, titled \"We Were All Born to Our Mothers\". Starting from September that year, tickets to their performances at various small venues would often sell out quickly;[\\[4\\]](#cite_note-4) subsequently their single \"Wimpish\" achieved over 180,000 views on YouTube following its release. The same year, they filmed their first music video \"Wayfarer\", in which Liu served as director.\\[*[citation needed](/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed \"Wikipedia:Citation needed\")*\\]\n\nIn 2016, the band released their first studio album, *The Servile*; shortly afterwards, it gained widespread attention among professional critics after they emerged as a dark horse in Taiwan's independent music scene.[\\[5\\]](#cite_note-5)[\\[6\\]](#cite_note-6)[\\[7\\]](#cite_note-7) On May 21, they held their second major concert \"We Were All Born to Our Mothers 2.0\", which marked the debut of drummer Fan Tsai after Liu left to focus on shooting music videos. Tsai, a childhood friend of Chan, was previously the drummer for post-rock band Triple Deer.[\\[8\\]](#cite_note-8) On October 29, they snatched three awards, including best band and best newcomer, at the 7th Golden Indie Music Awards.\\[*[citation needed](/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed \"Wikipedia:Citation needed\")*\\]\n\nOn June 24, 2017, the band won a total of three awards at the [28th Golden Melody Awards](/wiki/28th_Golden_Melody_Awards \"28th Golden Melody Awards\"), namely Best Musical Group, Best New Artist and Song of the Year for their song \"Simon Says\", the former in which they outperformed established acts such as [Mayday](/wiki/Mayday_\\(Taiwanese_band\\) \"Mayday (Taiwanese band)\").\\[*[citation needed](/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed \"Wikipedia:Citation needed\")*\\]\n\n### 2019–present: International success and Fan Tsai's death\n\n\\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=No_Party_for_Cao_Dong&action=edit&section=4 \"Edit section: 2019–present: International success and Fan Tsai's death\")\\]\n\nThe band played at [SXSW](/wiki/South_by_Southwest \"South by Southwest\") and [NXNE](/wiki/North_by_Northeast \"North by Northeast\") in 2019.[\\[9\\]](#cite_note-9)[\\[10\\]](#cite_note-10) They wrote and recorded the title song for the video game [Devotion](/wiki/Devotion_\\(video_game\\) \"Devotion (video game)\") by [Red Candle Games](/wiki/Red_Candle_Games \"Red Candle Games\") in 2019.[\\[11\\]](#cite_note-11)\n\nThe band had teased the release of new music with a livestream that would have begun on March 6, 2020. This however was cancelled, and their following album, which was planned for release in early 2020. was put on an indefinite delay due to the [COVID-19 pandemic](/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic \"COVID-19 pandemic\").\\[*[citation needed](/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed \"Wikipedia:Citation needed\")*\\]\n\nNo Party For Cao Dong hosted a livestream on their YouTube channel which took place once a day from May 20 to May 23 and featured live performers acting out a story, the course of which was chosen in real-time by the viewers in the chat, determining how the narrative would play out. At the end of the final episode on May 23, a new song was debuted while the credits rolled.[\\[12\\]](#cite_note-12)\n\nIn 2021, the band planned to hold their concert \"We Were All Born to Our Mothers 6.0\" for the first time at the [Taipei Arena](/wiki/Taipei_Arena \"Taipei Arena\") on May 22. Although 11,000 tickets were sold out in less than a minute, it was postponed indefinitely due to the COVID-19 pandemic.[\\[13\\]](#cite_note-13) On October 30, drummer Fan Tsai was found dead at the age of 26 at a quarantine hotel in Taipei City following the band's return from [Mainland China](/wiki/Mainland_China \"Mainland China\") where they conducted a concert tour. Her quarantine period was originally going to end on November 8, and homicide was ruled out as there was no foreign intrusion on the scene and no suicide note was left.[\\[14\\]](#cite_note-14) After much discussion, the remaining band members announced on November 25 that their \"We Were All Born to Our Mothers 6.0\" concert would be cancelled.\n\nThe band won three [Golden Melody Awards](/wiki/Golden_Melody_Awards \"Golden Melody Awards\"), for [Album of the Year](/wiki/Golden_Melody_Award_for_Album_of_the_Year \"Golden Melody Award for Album of the Year\"), [Best Mandarin Album](/wiki/Golden_Melody_Award_for_Best_Mandarin_Album \"Golden Melody Award for Best Mandarin Album\"), and [Best Band](/wiki/Golden_Melody_Award_for_Best_Band \"Golden Melody Award for Best Band\") in 2024, after releasing their second album, *The Clod*.[\\[15\\]](#cite_note-15)\n\n## Band members\n\n\\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=No_Party_for_Cao_Dong&action=edit&section=5 \"Edit section: Band members\")\\]\n\n**Current members**\n\n-   Wood Lin – lead guitar, vocals (2012–present)\n-   Judy Chan – rhythm guitar, vocals (2012–present)\n-   Sam Yang – bass guitar, vocals (2014–present; not touring since 2023)\n-   Huang Shih-wei – drums (2023–present)\n\n**Former members**\n\n-   Sam Cheng – bass guitar (2013–2014)\n-   Leo Liu – drums (2014–2016)\n-   Fan Tsai – drums (2016–2021; her death)\n\n**Touring substitutes**\n\n-   Dennis Chang – bass guitar, vocals (2023–present)\n\n### Timeline\n\n\\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=No_Party_for_Cao_Dong&action=edit&section=6 \"Edit \n（2016年）\n\n[瓦合](/wiki/%E7%93%A6%E5%90%88 \"瓦合\")  \n（2023年）\n\n收錄於《丑奴儿》的單曲\n\n1.  山海  \n    發行日期：2015年12月30日 (2015-12-30)\n2.  [大風吹](/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E9%A2%A8%E5%90%B9_\\(%E6%AD%8C%E6%9B%B2\\) \"大風吹 (歌曲)\")  \n    發行日期：2015年7月7日 (2015-07-07)\n\n《**醜奴兒**》（英語：*The Servile*）是[臺灣](/wiki/%E8%87%BA%E7%81%A3 \"臺灣\")[獨立搖滾](/wiki/%E7%8D%A8%E7%AB%8B%E6%90%96%E6%BB%BE \"獨立搖滾\")樂團[草東沒有派對](/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E6%9D%B1%E6%B2%92%E6%9C%89%E6%B4%BE%E5%B0%8D \"草東沒有派對\")的首張[錄音室專輯](/wiki/%E9%8C%84%E9%9F%B3%E5%AE%A4%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF \"錄音室專輯\")，2016年2月19日用于[The Orchard](/w/index.php?title=The_Orchard&action=edit&redlink=1 \"The Orchard（页面不存在）\")（英语：[The Orchard (company)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Orchard_\\(company\\) \"en:The Orchard (company)\")）和[Bandcamp](/wiki/Bandcamp \"Bandcamp\")發行數位專輯，[\\[5\\]](#cite_note-5)3月11日發行實体專輯。[\\[6\\]](#cite_note-:zy-6)最初发行的2000张实体唱片均为[手工制作](/wiki/%E7%A7%81%E5%88%B6%E5%94%B1%E7%89%87 \"私制唱片\")，仅在台湾11家[咖啡馆](/wiki/%E5%92%96%E5%95%A1%E9%A6%86 \"咖啡馆\")及独立唱片行发售，并在三天内售罄。[\\[7\\]](#cite_note-:02-7)\n\n专辑由製作人[李孝祖](/w/index.php?title=%E6%9D%8E%E5%AD%9D%E7%A5%96&action=edit&redlink=1 \"李孝祖（页面不存在）\")與乐队成員共同制作，曲风以[油渍摇滚](/wiki/%E6%B2%B9%E6%BC%AC%E6%90%96%E6%BB%BE \"油漬搖滾\")为主[\\[8\\]](#cite_note-:0-8)，融合了[后摇](/wiki/%E5%90%8E%E6%91%87 \"后摇\")、[金属](/wiki/%E9%87%8D%E9%87%91%E5%B1%9E%E9%9F%B3%E4%B9%90 \"重金属音乐\")、[朋克](/wiki/%E6%9C%8B%E5%85%8B%E6%91%87%E6%BB%9A \"朋克摇滚\")、[數學搖滾](/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E6%90%96%E6%BB%BE \"數學搖滾\")、[电子舞曲](/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E5%AD%90%E8%88%9E%E6%9B%B2 \"电子舞曲\")、[情绪摇滚](/wiki/%E6%83%85%E7%B7%92%E6%90%96%E6%BB%BE \"情緒搖滾\")等风格[\\[9\\]](#cite_note-:chow-9)[\\[10\\]](#cite_note-:4-10)以及受电子舞曲乐队[两门剧院乐队](/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%A4%E9%97%A8%E5%89%A7%E9%99%A2%E4%B9%90%E9%98%9F&action=edit&redlink=1 \"两门剧院乐队（页面不存在）\")（英语：[Two Door Cinema Club](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Two_Door_Cinema_Club \"en:Two Door Cinema Club\")）影响的传统摇滚[架构](/w/index.php?title=%E6%AD%8C%E6%9B%B2%E7%BB%93%E6%9E%84&action=edit&redlink=1 \"歌曲结构（页面不存在）\")（英语：[Song structure](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Song_structure \"en:Song structure\")），[\\[11\\]](#cite_note-11)[\\[12\\]](#cite_note-12)在專輯聲響中保留良好的動態，使聲音的情緒感更加充沛。歌词大多以年轻人的视角去表达对[社会不公](/wiki/%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E4%B8%8D%E5%B9%B3%E7%AD%89 \"社会不平等\")的批判，对未来的迷茫与自己的矛盾心理[\\[13\\]](#cite_note-:1-13)，引起了年轻人的共鸣，因此被乐评人贴上“鲁蛇世代”、“丧文化”代表的标签。[\\[7\\]](#cite_note-:02-7)[\\[8\\]](#cite_note-:0-8)[\\[13\\]](#cite_note-:1-13)\n\n此专辑的发布，引起了[台湾乐坛](/wiki/%E5%8F%B0%E7%81%A3%E9%9F%B3%E6%A8%82 \"台灣音樂\")的轰动，草东没有派对也成为台湾独立音乐圈不可忽视的黑马。[\\[14\\]](#cite_note-14)5月21日，乐队开始了第一次专辑巡演“不都妈生的2.0”，门票在十分钟内被抢空。[\\[15\\]](#cite_note-15)[\\[16\\]](#cite_note-:3-16)随着巡演消息发布的还有鼓手刘立因专注导演事业退团，新鼓手换为凡凡（蔡憶凡）。[\\[17\\]](#cite_note-17)[\\[18\\]](#cite_note-18)同年10月15日，草东在[脸书](/wiki/%E8%84%B8%E4%B9%A6 \"脸书\")宣布将进行“滔滔丙申年冬巡回”，大陆、台湾及北美场皆在短时间内售罄。[\\[16\\]](#cite_note-:3-16)[\\[19\\]](#cite_note-19)草東沒有派對以此張專輯入圍包括[第28屆金曲獎](/wiki/%E7%AC%AC28%E5%B1%86%E9%87%91%E6%9B%B2%E7%8D%8E \"第28屆金曲獎\")、[第7届金音奖](/wiki/%E7%AC%AC7%E5%B1%86%E9%87%91%E9%9F%B3%E7%8D%8E \"第7屆金音獎\")、第12届[KKBOX风云榜](/wiki/KKBOX%E9%A2%A8%E9%9B%B2%E6%A6%9C \"KKBOX風雲榜\")与首届[唱工委音乐奖](/wiki/%E5%94%B1%E5%B7%A5%E5%A7%94%E9%9F%B3%E4%B9%90%E5%A5%96 \"唱工委音乐奖\")等多项音乐奖项，其中专辑在第28届金曲奖的表现尤为耀眼，共入围6项，获奖3项，成为媒体公认的“最大赢家”。評審主席[黃韻玲](/wiki/%E9%BB%83%E9%9F%BB%E7%8E%B2 \"黃韻玲\")表示：「他們是悶世代的爆發。音樂給人太大的衝擊，打破大家對於聽覺的想法。」[\\[20\\]](#cite_note-20)[\\[21\\]](#cite_note-21)[\\[22\\]](#cite_note-22)\n\n## 背景与制作\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=1 \"编辑章节：背景与制作\")\\]\n\n参见：[草东没有派对](/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E6%9D%B1%E6%B2%92%E6%9C%89%E6%B4%BE%E5%B0%8D \"草東沒有派對\")\n\n[![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/CaoDong_St._Intersection.jpg/250px-CaoDong_St._Intersection.jpg)](/wiki/File:CaoDong_St._Intersection.jpg)\n\n位于[阳明山](/wiki/%E9%98%B3%E6%98%8E%E5%B1%B1 \"阳明山\")脚下的[草东街](/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E6%9D%B1%E8%A1%97 \"草東街\")是“草东没有派对”团名的来源，也是成员汲取灵感的地方\n\n2012年，同为高中同学并且同样爱好[摇滚乐](/wiki/%E6%91%87%E6%BB%9A%E4%B9%90 \"摇滚乐\")的巫堵（林耕佑）与已休学一年的筑筑（詹为筑）在[草东街](/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E6%9D%B1%E8%A1%97 \"草東街\")偶然重遇，此后他们经常在草东街讨论摇滚乐，并在此建立了乐团，命名为“草东街左转”，[\\[23\\]](#cite_note-23)后改为“草东街派对”，巫堵担任[主唱](/wiki/%E4%B8%BB%E5%94%B1 \"主唱\")兼节奏[吉他手](/wiki/%E5%90%89%E4%BB%96%E6%89%8B \"吉他手\")，筑筑担任主音吉他手。[\\[24\\]](#cite_note-24)后因乐队成员的几次变更，便将团名改为“草东没有派对”。[\\[25\\]](#cite_note-25)\n\n2014年，草东没有派对在[YouTube](/wiki/YouTube \"YouTube\")与[街聲](/wiki/%E8%A1%97%E8%81%B2 \"街聲\")发布了《五十》、《老张》、《丑》等作品，引起乐迷关注。[\\[2\\]](#cite_note-:2-2)2014年，在[贝斯手](/wiki/%E8%B4%9D%E6%96%AF%E6%89%8B \"贝斯手\")郑敬儒（现[deca joins](/wiki/Deca_joins \"Deca joins\")吉他手兼主唱）因被征召服[兵役](/wiki/%E5%8F%B0%E6%B9%BE%E5%85%B5%E5%BD%B9%E5%88%B6%E5%BA%A6 \"台湾兵役制度\")而离团后，[\\[26\\]](#cite_note-26)[\\[27\\]](#cite_note-27)乐队停摆一年。在乐队长达一年的停摆期间，乐队成员开始转变态度并认真创作，曲风也从原受[两门剧院乐队](/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%A4%E9%97%A8%E5%89%A7%E9%99%A2%E4%B9%90%E9%98%9F&action=edit&redlink=1 \"两门剧院乐队（页面不存在）\")（英语：[Two Door Cinema Club](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Two_Door_Cinema_Club \"en:Two Door Cinema Club\")）影响颇深的[电子舞曲](/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E5%AD%90%E8%88%9E%E6%9B%B2 \"电子舞曲\")转变为类似[涅槃乐队](/wiki/%E6%B6%85%E6%A7%83%E4%B9%90%E9%98%9F \"涅槃乐队\")的[油渍摇滚](/wiki/%E6%B2%B9%E6%BC%AC%E6%90%96%E6%BB%BE \"油漬搖滾\")。直到巫堵从[国立台北艺术大学](/wiki/%E5%9C%8B%E7%AB%8B%E5%8F%B0%E5%8C%97%E8%97%9D%E8%A1%93%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8 \"國立台北藝術大學\")“摇滚研究社”邀请新贝斯手世暄（杨世暄）与[鼓手](/wiki/%E9%BC%93%E6%89%8B \"鼓手\")刘立（刘承杰）加入乐团，筑筑找来高中同学赵若君做乐队经纪人。[\\[28\\]](#cite_note-28)[\\[29\\]](#cite_note-p2-29)至此，乐队阵容便稳定了下来。与此同时，独立制作人[李孝祖](/w/index.php?title=%E6%9D%8E%E5%AD%9D%E7%A5%96&action=edit&redlink=1 \"李孝祖（页面不存在）\")经朋友介绍听了乐队的几首歌曲后，决定与乐队合伙制作他们的[手工](/wiki/%E7%A7%81%E5%88%B6%E5%94%B1%E7%89%87 \"私制唱片\")同名[EP](/wiki/EP \"EP\")《草东没有派对》。阵容稳定后，2015年5月20日，草东带着第一场大型音乐会“不都妈生的”作为复出首场，并且在巡演过程中售卖他们的EP，从9月份开始，乐队巡演开始变得一票难求，100张限量EP也被抢空，收录在EP中的作品陆续被乐迷上传至YouTube，其中《[大风吹](/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E9%A2%A8%E5%90%B9_\\(%E6%AD%8C%E6%9B%B2\\) \"大風吹 (歌曲)\")》在不到半年时间内突破九万五千次[点击量](/wiki/%E9%BB%9E%E6%93%8A%E9%87%8F \"點擊量\")，[\\[2\\]](#cite_note-:2-2)并在一年内突破五十万点击量。[\\[30\\]](#cite_note-30)\n\n2015年11月，在申请获得了[中华民国文化部](/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%B0%91%E5%9B%BD%E6%96%87%E5%8C%96%E9%83%A8 \"中华民国文化部\")三十万[新台币](/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E5%8F%B0%E5%B8%81 \"新台币\")的“硬地樂團專輯錄製補助”后，[\\[31\\]](#cite_note-:roc-31)草东没有派对与李孝祖合作，开始在李孝祖创办的“好意思录音室”开始录制新专辑，并在12月接受媒体采访时宣布新专辑的名字为《丑奴儿》。[\\[2\\]](#cite_note-:2-2)专辑名取自宋代词人[辛弃疾](/wiki/%E8%BE%9B%E5%BC%83%E7%96%BE \"辛弃疾\")的《[丑奴儿·书博山道中壁](https://zh.wikisource.org/wiki/%E9%87%87%E6%A1%91%E5%AD%90_\\(%E8%BE%9B%E5%BC%83%E7%96%BE\\) \"s:采桑子 (辛弃疾)\")》之[词牌名](/wiki/%E8%A9%9E%E7%89%8C%E5%90%8D \"詞牌名\")“[丑奴儿](/wiki/%E9%87%87%E6%A1%91%E5%AD%90 \"采桑子\")”，用词中名句暗中自嘲乐队“少年不识愁滋味”“为赋新词强说愁”。[\\[32\\]](#cite_note-32)专辑录制工作基本结束。[\\[33\\]](#cite_note-33)经过混音师Andy Baker的混音工作与Joel Hatstat负责母带后制后，专辑制作完成。[\\[1\\]](#cite_note-:sci-1)\n\n## 歌曲和主题\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=2 \"编辑章节：歌曲和主题\")\\]\n\n[![[icon]](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png)](/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg)\n\n此章节需要[**扩充**](https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit)。\n\n全专辑词曲在专辑文案中由草东没有派对成员集体创作，但歌词主要为巫堵所创。 第一首《Intro》是专辑的[序曲](/wiki/%E5%BA%8F%E6%9B%B2 \"序曲\")，为纯器乐演奏。开场的《Intro》《丑》《烂泥》为一首[组曲](/wiki/%E7%BB%84%E6%9B%B2 \"组曲\")：《丑》\n\n## 发行\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=3 \"编辑章节：发行\")\\]\n\n[![[icon]](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png)](/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg)\n\n此章节需要[**扩充**](https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit)。\n\n## 曲目\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=4 \"编辑章节：曲目\")\\]\n\n全碟词曲：草東沒有派對　全碟编曲：草東沒有派對　全碟製作人：李孝祖[\\[4\\]](#cite_note-Tidal-4)　\n\n曲序\n\n曲目\n\n备注\n\n时长\n\n1.\n\nIntro\n\n純音樂\n\n1:27\n\n2.\n\n醜（Grisly Me）\n\n \n\n1:58\n\n3.\n\n爛泥（Wimpish）\n\n《[麻醉風暴2](/wiki/%E9%BA%BB%E9%86%89%E9%A2%A8%E6%9A%B42 \"麻醉風暴2\")》主題曲\n\n2:30\n\n4.\n\n勇敢的人（The Reluctant）\n\n \n\n3:41\n\n5.\n\n[大風吹](/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E9%A2%A8%E5%90%B9_\\(%E6%AD%8C%E6%9B%B2\\) \"大風吹 (歌曲)\")（Simon Says）\n\n \n\n3:56\n\n6.\n\n艾瑪（Emma）\n\n \n\n3:22\n\n7.\n\n等（Await）\n\n \n\n2:36\n\n8.\n\n鬼（The Specter）\n\n \n\n2:40\n\n9.\n\n在（Am for You）\n\n \n\n4:40\n\n10.\n\n山海（Wayfarer）\n\n \n\n4:11\n\n11.\n\n我們（Us）\n\n \n\n3:39\n\n12.\n\n情歌（Mottos, Bygones）\n\n \n\n4:17\n\n总时长：\n\n38:57\n\n## 巡演\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=5 \"编辑章节：巡演\")\\]\n\n[![[icon]](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png)](/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg)\n\n此章节需要[**扩充**](https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit)。\n\n### 不都妈生的2.0\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=6 \"编辑章节：不都妈生的2.0\")\\]\n\n### 滔滔丙申年冬巡回\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=7 \"编辑章节：滔滔丙申年冬巡回\")\\]\n\n## 反响\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=8 \"编辑章节：反响\")\\]\n\n[![[icon]](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png)](/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg)\n\n此章节需要[**扩充**](https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit)。\n\n## 得獎紀錄\n\n\\[[编辑](/w/index.php?title=%E9%86%9C%E5%A5%B4%E5%85%92_\\(%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF\\)&action=edit&section=9 \"编辑章节：得獎紀錄\")\\]\n\n**2016年[第7屆金音獎](/wiki/%E7%AC%AC7%E5%B1%86%E9%87%91%E9%9F%B3%E7%8D%8E contributor《空》是草东没有派对2023年发行专辑《瓦合》的第二首歌曲。通过深刻的歌词与带有强烈表达性的电吉他和鼓点，这首歌充分表达了一种对于虚无的无奈，反抗，和接受。\n\n《空》并非为《瓦合》写的歌曲，而是在鼓手凡凡去世之前撰写的许多歌曲之一。因此，它与专辑名称对应，并不是一首应该与其他歌曲连贯的歌。Expand ShareQ&amp;AFind answers to
